Each row in this table represents an event in which an entity (customer/ store staff) registration takes place.  It captures information like the channel where the profile was created; the type of entity registered; date and time of the registration; and the store identifier for the registration.

**Databricks Table Name:** registration\_event

**Registration Event - Entity Relationship Diagram (ERD)**

Zoom in the table for more clarity. Click the table title to view its details.

**Registration Event Fact Table**

<Table align={[null,"center",null,"center","center"]}>
  <thead>
    <tr>
      <th>
        **Column Name**
      </th>

      <th>
        **Data Type**
      </th>

      <th>
        **Description**
      </th>

      <th>
        <Glossary>Linked Table</Glossary>
      </th>

      <th>
        **Availability for Export in the[Registration Event Log](https://docs.capillarytech.com/docs/registration-event-standard-export-template) Template**
      </th>
    </tr>
  </thead>

  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <td>
        activity
      </td>

      <td>
        string
      </td>

      <td>
        Specifies the source activity that triggered the registration event. Possible values are - wechat\_follow, wechat\_register, tmall\_register, system, website\_register, ecommerce\_register, and jd\_register.
      </td>

      <td>
        \_
      </td>

      <td>
        Yes; Measure Name: Activity
      </td>
    </tr>

    <tr>
      <td>
        auto\_update\_time\_entity\_life\_cycle
      </td>

      <td>
        bigint
      </td>

      <td>
        Date and time when the corresponding record in the entity life cycle table available at the source was last updated. It is in the Unix timestamp format.
      </td>

      <td>
        \_
      </td>

      <td>
        Yes; Measure Name: Auto Update Time Entity Life Cycle
      </td>
    </tr>

    <tr>
      <td>
        dim\_channel\_account\_id
      </td>

      <td>
        bigint
      </td>

      <td>
        Identifier for the channel where the customer's profile was created. Possible values are - Whatsapp, Web\_engage, Mobile\_app, Line, and WeChat.
      </td>

      <td>
        [channel\_account](https://docs.capillarytech.com/docs/dimension-tables#channel-account)
      </td>

      <td>
        Yes; Dimension Name: Channel Account > Channel Account Id
      </td>
    </tr>

    <tr>
      <td>
        dim\_entity\_type\_id
      </td>

      <td>
        bigint
      </td>

      <td>
        Identifier for the entity type. Possible values are - Customer, and Store staff.
      </td>

      <td>
        [entity\_type](https://docs.capillarytech.com/docs/dimension-tables#entity-type)
      </td>

      <td>
        Yes; Dimension Name: Entity Type > Id
      </td>
    </tr>

    <tr>
      <td>
        dim\_event\_date\_id
      </td>

      <td>
        bigint
      </td>

      <td>
        Date when the registration was done.
      </td>

      <td>
        [date](https://docs.capillarytech.com/docs/dimension-tables#date)
      </td>

      <td>
        Yes; Dimension Name: Date > Date
      </td>
    </tr>

    <tr>
      <td>
        dim\_event\_time\_id
      </td>

      <td>
        bigint
      </td>

      <td>
        Time when the registration was done.
      </td>

      <td>
        [time](https://docs.capillarytech.com/docs/dimension-tables#time)
      </td>

      <td>
        Yes; Dimension Name: Time > Time
      </td>
    </tr>

    <tr>
      <td>
        dim\_event\_user\_id
      </td>

      <td>
        bigint
      </td>

      <td>
        Identifier of the customer who has registered. It is an internally assigned value by Capillary for user identification.
      </td>

      <td>
        [users](https://docs.capillarytech.com/docs/dimension-tables#users-users)
      </td>

      <td>
        Yes; Dimension Name: User > User Id
      </td>
    </tr>

    <tr>
      <td>
        dim\_event\_zone\_till\_id
      </td>

      <td>
        bigint
      </td>

      <td>
        Identifier assigned to the point-of-sale (POS) terminal within a store. It distinguishes one checkout location from another within the same store, aiding in transaction tracking and management.
      </td>

      <td>
        [zone till](https://docs.capillarytech.com/docs/dimension-tables#zone-till)
      </td>

      <td>
        Yes; Dimension Name: Store Hierarchy > Till Id
      </td>
    </tr>

    <tr>
      <td>
        dim\_latest\_updated\_date\_id
      </td>

      <td>
        bigint
      </td>

      <td>
        Date when the data corresponding to this event/row is changed in the source table.
      </td>

      <td>
        [date](https://docs.capillarytech.com/docs/dimension-tables#date)
      </td>

      <td>
        Yes; Dimension Name: Latest Updated Date > Date

      <td>
        dim\_latest\_updated\_time\_id
      </td>

      <td>
        bigint
      </td>

      <td>

      </td>

      <td>
        [time](https://docs.capillarytech.com/docs/dimension-tables#time)
      </td>

      <td>
        Yes; Dimension Name: Latest Updated Time > Time Id

    <tr>
      <td>
        dim\_state\_id
      </td>

      <td>
        bigint
      </td>

      <td>
        Identifier of the status of the registration. Possible values are - Completed, executing, int\_wait, failed, queued, temporary failure, and ext\_wait.
      </td>

      <td>
        [state](https://docs.capillarytech.com/docs/dimension-tables#state)
      </td>

      <td>
        Yes; Dimension Name: State > Id
      </td>
    </tr>

    <tr>
      <td>
        id
      </td>

      <td>
        bigint
      </td>

      <td>
        Unique identifier of the table. It is the primary key of the table.
      </td>

      <td>
        \_
      </td>

      <td>
        Yes; Measure Name: Id
      </td>
    </tr>

    <tr>
      <td>
        reference\_id
      </td>

      <td>
        string
      </td>

      <td>
        Represents the request\_id of the API call that resulted in the creation of this entity. For example, it could be the requestId from a customer update call. This is the primary key for this table.
      </td>

      <td>
        \_
      </td>

      <td>
        Yes; Measure Name: Reference Id
      </td>
    </tr>

    <tr>
      <td>
        registration\_event\_rank
      </td>

      <td>
        bigint
      </td>

      <td>
        This field is computed on the Enhanced Insights side.
      </td>

      <td>
        \_
      </td>

      <td>
        Yes; Measure Name: Registration Event Rank
      </td>
    </tr>

    <tr>
      <td>
        year
      </td>

      <td>
        int
      </td>

      <td>
        Year of registration.
      </td>

      <td>
        \_
      </td>

      <td>
        Yes; Dimension Name: Year
      </td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</Table>
